Step 67, training acc: 0.420, instruction: Time is a complicated concept. It can be measured in seconds, minutes, hours, days, weeks, months, and years. Today is the day after yesterday and the day before tomorrow. This pattern continues indefinitely, and we can use it to calculate the date one day ago. To do so, simply subtract one from the date of today. In other words, the date one day ago is today minus one.

Step 145, training acc: 0.440, instruction: 
Step 145, training acc: 0.360, instruction: A leap year is a year with 366 days instead of 365 days. It occurs every 4 years, except when the year ends in two 0s (for example, 1900, 1904, 2000 were not leap years). Leap years occur when the Earth rotates around the Sun once in its orbit. As a result of this leap year, February 2024 was a leap month, and Jane and John got married on February 29th.

Step 196, training acc: 0.440, instruction: The UK follows a different date format from the US. In the UK, the date is written in the order of day, month, and year. So, in the UK, 02/01/1987 would be written as 01/02/1987. Therefore, the date one year ago from today in the MM/DD/YYYY format would be 01/02/1986.
